Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer: lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	We have already described in the division the appearances of dropsy, and how the gathering of fluid is caused, and the signs of each appearance, and the treatment by medicine, and that which is cured by iron; only these two cases are mentioned: tympany and hydrops, for they are fatal conditions. Therefore, when you treat this form of dropsy called "tympany" with medicines, and the cure does not help, then consider whether the patient is weak, or has another illness besides dropsy, such as a swollen stomach and similar conditions; in that case, do not use iron, for there is danger in it. But if you see the patient is very strong, and has only dropsy, and is neither too young nor too old, then proceed thus: raise the patient upright on your hands, and have an assistant press his abdomen to force the fluid down to the lowest part of the feet. Then take a spatha with a pointed end, according to this shape:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let there be two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier; puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu; puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	And let there be two parts. a point, and yet not so sharp that it can reach the intestines when it is inserted, nor cause bleeding; then examine whether the dropsy is in the intestines: if you should split below the navel on the right side of the abdomen three fingers deep; and if the dropsy is due to liver disease, then split on the left side of the abdomen three fingers; and if it is due to the spleen, then split on the right, and the patient must not lie on the split so that the excess fluids do not flow into that weak area; then pierce all the way through the skin with the instrument, and squeeze it, and remove your hand from the entire spatulum between the skin and the syphon as you would when skinning a finger or toe; then pierce the syphon until the fluid emerges at the desired location, and that is where the water is, then pull it out, and insert this instrument again with which there is the shape:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus; et II d’autre part, et I d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	It resembles a slender silver needle, and is made of lightweight bronze or brass, with a small hole in the lower part. On one side there are three holes, on another two, and on the third, one; the head is shaped like a feather, and this is the form of the incision that scribes make when they sharpen feathers:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort; mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit; fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	at the top is the vent hole, so that when the instrument comes into contact with the wound, it will release water immediately onto the wound; therefore empty out half or a third of the amount, for if you empty more than is appropriate in that hour, by chance the patient may die from the shock of the instrument, or he will faint, or he will come close to death; but empty it according to the quantity of his strength and according to what the disposition of his strength signifies, and his pulses; then withdraw the instrument and retain the water, and it is retained now by the membrane which blocks the hole that is above the syphon, about which I have spoken, that you pierce in this manner; then reintroduce the instrument the next day, if you see the patient bearing this, and withdraw a little amount of water; do this every day, and beware of fooling around until it no longer holds but just a bit of water.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre; et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	And if you doubt the illness, then leave him in water for a long time, and apply a poultice of hot sand or warm mud, and through much sweating or bathing, and in the sun, and let him drink tinting liquids; and treat with medicines that dry up the humors until he is healed, and cauterize the stomach and liver and spleen after the extraction of the water, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the stopping of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without a foreskin, or with a small foreskin, or one that is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If necessary, cut into the foreskin with a very thin knife according to this method:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	Then place a slender plug of wood in the foreskin, and tie it there, and keep it like that for three or four days, and when he wants to urinate, remove the plug, and he will be able to urinate, and then replace the plug; sometimes this is not necessary because the urine that comes out pushes aside the foreskin.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	Those whose foreskin is small, if they are circumcised with a sharp knife, as we have said, will enlarge.

Those who do not have the foreskin in its place are defective, for some are born with the foreskin at the tip of the penis, which prevents them from urinating unless they lift their penis upwards; and they cannot copulate because the material cannot reach the bladder, and this is a serious ailment.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the way to treat it is for the patient to lie on his back, then the head and glans of the penis are raised up like a feather, as thick as a pen, so that the opening is in the middle, as it should be; and beware of bleeding which often occurs there, and if it does, stanch the flow with something that stops blood, and cure the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of pustules on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many times this albata occurs on the penis, and it is an ugly-looking growth; there are both malignant and non-malignant types; therefore you must take them with a small, sharp knife, cut them and clean them all, then put wet cotton in Egyptian ointment on top; then cure with thin ointment until they are healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, discolored and putrid, then you must apply cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	When you have cut it, and if the ulcer is on the shaft of the penis, and part of it is inside and part outside, then you must first remove the ulcer that is inside; and when it is healed, then cure the outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because when you treat it together, if the scrotum is not secured so that it is not pierced, and blackness and corruption come to his penis and testicles; then everything that is black and rotten must be cut off, then bind it with the ointment of honey and flour made from pomegranate rind and fennel, then treat it with other treatments until it heals.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if there is bleeding, use the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars; et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	The cauteries help in two ways together: that is, for bleeding and corruption; and if the scrotum is swollen and retracted, you must insert a hollow cane into the penis, and the patient must urinate through it; and when there is hair at the tip of the penis which happens to those who have not been circumcised, either because of a wound or an abscess, then you must scrape away the skin with an instrument, as far as the hair, and loosen the scrotum all around, and free the penis from all parts; and if it is a difficult thing to discuss, then you must scrape it with a spatulum made of wood at the tip of the penis and the foreskin; then gently pull them apart and put a thin damp linen cloth between them in cold water so that it does not swell again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not a matter of continence like other wounds; nevertheless, when we perform this act of our own will, and properly on infants, it is necessary that we make the best and lightest cut for their salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not mention the circumcision of their infants, for they did not practice it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For I have seen most of the masters and surgeons who perform circumcision all around the foreskin, some forcefully, and on all new borns; thus, the head of the penis would become inflamed as there are two membranes, and by chance one gets pushed upwards while the other remains underneath.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Then they cover it again, and the pain becomes doubled, and at the purification which is done on the foreskin isn't secured the tip of the member; and at the purification of the nail sometimes the cautery slips and ruins the work, and many times they are born such that they don't need purification, and I have seen this.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the purification that is done forcefully all around the thread of hair, I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut justly both above and below.

Because when you press your hand, you cut evenly in all directions; but the thread should be wrapped tightly around the skin; and the method of the first operation is that you make the child think that you are only tying the thread around the rod, and then you should pull it in every way you can; then hold it straight between your hands, and press down on the forces between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments; then put your hand to the rod and breathe into the wound, and draw it up until the head of the rod is in; then cleanse it well from the dirt that has accumulated there, then tie the place with a double thread, then tie it under the other end; and hold it with both hands by the second binding, at the foreskin and the index finger, and press between the two bindings, then lift the skin gently and pull the head of the rod; then let the blood flow little by little, because that is the wound; and put powder on top of the powder, and cover it with a piece of cloth glued with an egg cooked in rose water, confited with good and fresh rosemary oil, and leave it until the next day, and cure it with other cures until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The shape of the forces for purification is as follows: both heads should be tense and pointed, and the heads should be as large as the palm equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	the error of purification is when the pus within the incision has dried up; therefore, you must extend it with your nail, so that the pus forms an abscess; and then cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your nail, hold it with tweezers and then cut.

dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division; et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e; et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The retention of urine is due to the obstruction of a stone, or congealed blood, or a tumor, or similar conditions, as we have said in our discussion of these matters. If the urine is not released and you see that it is being retained by a stone lodged in the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent forward at the waist, with his feet placed on his back and his abdomen pressed down from above the waist, and he should strain as hard as he can. This will force the neck of the bladder upwards, causing the stone to pass and the urine to flow; if it does not, as we have said, and the patient experiences great pain, then you must apply suction with an instrument called a "syringe," which is crafted as follows: it should be made of fine silver, as light as a bird's feather, with a length of one and a half palms, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede; puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine; et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And the manner of urination is that you take a double thread and tie it to the tip of some wool or cotton, and insert the tip of the thread into the syringe; and squeeze out the excess wool and insert it into the syringe up to the root of the penis, then lubricate the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and have the patient sit on a chair, and raise the bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water; then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the body; then fill the syringe up to the bladder, and feel the patient urinate until the bladder is empty, and if this is not done in this order, it is because the person guiding the syringe is doing it wrong; then pull out the thread through all the wool, and the urine will follow the wool; then remove the thread, and let the urine flow; and repeat the syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of diseases of the bladder:
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When burns or blood come in the bladder, or pus is accumulated there, and you see water and medicine distilling, then do this to all of the instrument that is called "clepsydra", and it is formed:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus: II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est; et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	It is closed and has three openings: two on one side and one on the other, as you can see. The suitable medicine to shorten the urethra without addition, so that moisture can be drawn out and pushed in when necessary; and when you see your medicine moving within the bladder, place the end of the catheter in the moisture and draw it up to where it is, thus drawing the moisture into the catheter; then push strongly on the catheter, allowing the moisture to enter. Now it will go into the bladder and the patient will feel it; this is the form of the subtle catheter with which they catheterize the bladder: so it is made:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie; et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And it is made of silver or bronze, and has the head higher up, and below are two strings attached to it; then take a sheep's bladder and put in it the moisture with which you want to catheterize the bladder, then tie the two strings formed from a strong thread together, and heat this moisture over fire; then insert the end of the catheter into the urethra, then hold your hand over the bladder and squeeze gently until all the moisture goes into the bladder so that the patient feels it. And if you don't have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make a circle of it, piercing it with a hole around; then thread the strong thread through these holes, then assemble the circle as one assembles a wheel, and put inside what you want of oil, moisture, and water, and tie it in the instrument. Then do as you did with the bladder, squeezing with your hand until all the moisture goes into the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division the methods of stone extraction, along with medicines; and I have said the difference between a stone lodged in the urethra, and all the signs, and in which type of stone one should operate on cutting; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that the urine exits from the bladder resembling water in its subtlety; and it opens up like an onion, and the patient feels pain in his penis, and he can urinate many times, and then it blocks again; and many of these stones cause a fundament; and the healing is easier for children until they are four years old, and it is very serious in the elderly, and it is intermediate in those who are between youth and old age; and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is fitting first to cleanse the patient through enema, to draw out all the feces which are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes blocks the search for the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	Then take the patient by the feet and raise him up and move him about, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from above; then let him sit between your hands, with his arms underneath his thighs, so that the bladder is completely bent downward; then examine and feel inside; if you sense the stone in the space, then hasten now to cut upon the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	And if it does not come out with the touch, then moisten your left index finger with oil, if the patient is old, or your middle finger, if the patient is young; and insert it into its anus, and examine the stone, and when you sense it with your finger, then draw it to the neck of the bladder; then press upon your finger and draw out the stone from where you see to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the minister to press the bladder with his hand, and tell him to extend his fingers up with his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin under the testicles in the area where one performs the incision; then he fills the spatulum, which is the mold.
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And cut between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the side of the left buttock; and be straight on the stone, and your toes be next to the anus, and let the incision be diagonal so that it is wide at the top and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large; by chance, the pressure on the toe which is at the anus may cause it to pop out without any effort; and know that there is a kind of stone in which there are angles and edges: it is difficult to extract; and there is another kind which is below, resembling a grape, and round, whose extraction is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole; et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	For those with angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not pop out, you should grip it with tweezers that are like a file at the tip, to extract the stone so that it doesn't escape; or you insert a tube under it, which is thin at the tip; and if you cannot grab it thus, then widen the opening, and if there is no blood, then crush it with vitriol; and if there is more than one stone, then first insert the largest into the neck of the bladder, then push it in, then pull out the one further up, and the smaller ones after if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be seared, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	For two things happen to the patient: either he dies or urine escapes through the opening where the urethra cannot heal; but nevertheless strive to pull it, or scrape with tongs until you have pulled it apart in pieces; and when you have finished your work, use incense and myrrh and dragon's blood on the wound, and constrict it, and put over it a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or in oil and rosewater and cold water to soothe the hot abscess; then rebind the injury around his neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the area well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And if hot abscesses and scorching and blood congealing in the bladder, and urine is retained as a result, all of which is perceived in such a way that it emerges with the urine: then press your finger into the wound and draw out that blood, for if any remains, the bladder will be harmed and burst; then wash the wound with water and garlic and salt, and treat him in every way you know until he is healed; and it is fitting that each time you treat him, you bind his two thighs together and apply remedies to the area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	And if the stone is small and lodged in the urethra and embedded there, and the urine cannot pass; then the treatment I have described above, which you should cut many times, is an excuse for not cutting during this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have tried this before.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take an iron needle with three pointed ends and insert it into a hot brand:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis under the stone so that it cannot move back into the bladder; then push the needle into the penis gently until it reaches the stone; then turn the needle in your hand within the stone a little bit at a time, until you can pierce the stone from another side; then urine will flow immediately, then press your hand on what is left of the stone inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is broken at once and comes out with the urine, then the patient is cured; and if you cannot do this for any reason that they are resistant, then tie a thread under the stone and another above, then spread the penis over the stone between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the string, and cleanse the congealed blood in the wound; and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone is lodged in women's bodies, and if it does, the cure is difficult due to three reasons: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; the second is that one cannot find a skilled female healer who can be trusted, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And the third way is that by chance one cannot find a woman well skilled in this art of midwifery; and the fourth way is that the woman's stone is more deeply embedded than a man's, so it requires a deeper incision, and there is great fear involved. And if necessity arises, one should take a midwife who is very knowledgeable, and with difficulty persuade her, and if one cannot persuade her, then one should use a very subtle cast; and present to her a wise old woman experienced in the life of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and instruct her to do what you command regarding the examination of the stone. And be sure to examine carefully whether the woman is a virgin: then she should insert her finger into the vagina and look for the stone; and if she finds it, she should press it beneath her finger, and recommend that she inserts her finger into the vagina where the pain is, and press her left hand firmly over the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	If she has a hernia, she should move it gradually from the bladder to below, until it reaches the root of the thigh; then press on the stone at the root of the thigh towards the middle, where there is movement in the part where you feel the stone; do not move your finger over the stone or underneath it, and make the incision small at first. Then stitch up the incision if you feel the stone has been cut so that it can come out; know that there are many types of stones: small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and some with hair on them.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	you will know what to look for in order to identify the type of stone.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood comes out, apply ground vitriol and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your task and remove the stone, having prepared the instruments I have described for extracting stones in men, to assist you in your work. And if the blood flows and it is from an artery that has been cut, apply the powder to the site and use bandages and tourniquets, and do not re-open it; leave the stone and do not attempt to remove it, lest the patient die; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, return to your work so that the stone comes out.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Ramice aquouse is nothing other than an accumulation of moisture or white pus, which is located under the heart of the testicles, within the egg; and it is called "pus," and sometimes it is properly located in the membrane of the egg, if one believes that it is not the same egg.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ramice is due to weakness that comes to the testicles and is spread out from there.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors: or it is yellowish, or red-free, or black, or watery white, and so on; and these are the signs by which we recognize this disorder. For if it is in the white syphilis that we have mentioned, then the abscesses are soft, as long as a fig, and do not burst the testicles, for there is moisture all around them.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	If there is moisture in the testicle itself, then the abscess is soft with part of an egg, and because of this one thinks it is another egg; and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white syphilis, then one feels it well. So when you want to know the color of the moisture, test all over the scrotum, from which the shape is described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then, what comes after the insertion point, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when we treat it with iron, the patient should be healed according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he should lie on his back on something slightly raised, and have a lot of sheets underneath him; then he should sit up on his left side, and instruct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs of the heart; then take the lit spatula, and cut the skin of the ribs between them from the long end down to the armpit, and the incision should be straight as you cut the skin of the ribs up to the white part of the shoulder blade, and cut it carefully according to your strength; then pierce the acromion plain with water through a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then put in your fingers, and raise the acromion upwards; and do not touch the heart, but only the acromion; cut all around it carefully, just as you cut the ribcage, or the water will return; and if the egg leaps out during your work, return it to its place when you have finished the work of the acromion; then bring together the two edges of the heart with a stitch, then treat the wound as the others, until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, then you must tie off the suspended vessels, fearing the flow of blood; then cut open the scrotum throughout its suspension, extract the egg, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	If the water is collected in two parts together, know that these are two haggles; then press the other part as you did the first one equally, then wash off the blood, and put on the wound soft lamb's wool soaked in rose oil; and put into another lamb's wool moistened with wine and oil, and place it over both haggles, and place doubled-up sheets on top, and bind it up all along the line which is according to this form.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take two sheets and fill them with wool according to this appearance, and have them sewn together at the crotch of the breeches; and one of the heads presses upon the fundament up to the back, and the other on the part of the armpit; and the other two heads upon the two angles, and all the binding is made in the buckle of the breeches; and sometimes this haggle is treated by cautery instead of an incision with a knife; and one takes a thin scalpel, and cuts the skin of the haggles, and it is scorched as we have said so that the white sac containing water is uncovered; then take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that sac at the joints, and scorch it with this thin hot cautery.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And the cup in every way that you can, as long as you stretch everything out; and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this work is safest; and move carefully to prevent blood flow, and changes in the wounds of the incision; and if nothing makes you do the opposite, either in abscesses or blood flow or anything else, then cure what makes you do the opposite, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit; pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this treatment because of its horror, then administer perforation as I have told you, and when you are certain by the signs that we have mentioned that the water is gone, then let the patient sit on a high seat; then pierce the abscess in the part below all the way to the lung, and place the perforation deep into the body; and make the holes wide so that all the fluid flows out; then put cotton over the wound and tie it, and let the remaining fluid flow out, then cure the wound until it is healed; and if the white membrane does not allow the fluid to exit through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to treat dropsy patients, of which the shape is described earlier; and make the wound larger, and know that the fluid will return and collect again after six months or so, and when it has collected as before, the patient will recover.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse; et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	Know that in the incision of this branch there are many dispositions of fear, because of which it seems better to leave it, and I will tell you the work and appearances of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I say therefore that many abscesses come in the body, especially in the testicles; and it is because of various causes.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	This is to be known by an acute surplus and ague, which is spread to the bowels, or from a blow; and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body; and it does not hurt, and it is a serious abscess; and sometimes there are gray, fearful, and fleshy abscesses, and a flowing color, and at times it comes from an artery, or from inflammation of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	When it is from an artery, it is known by the hot disposition of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers; and you must not touch it.Et s’il est de voine, il est conus par coldure et blance, ou de nout d’artere, si est conus par color de sang.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	Those who are affected by swelling of the vein are known by their appearance and the feel of the testicles, and one can correctly make the incision on this basis, and on other similar cases; you should cut the scrotum, then the testicles will be above, and the white substance will be exposed, and the suspensory ligament of the testicle will be freed from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	If the testicle is already damaged by these diseases, then you must cut it and cop it; and if it is gangrenous in the scrotum or in what is inside the vessels, then you must free all that membrane and cop it roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the crack is at the back of the shell, then you must crack it all and extract the egg as we have said.Et s’il y a u neuue char ou dedens la tenve, si covient que tu la cope et la delivre, et mets l’uef en autre vaissel.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is done, then dress the wound with soft wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it heals.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	This is a kind of abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to a plum, with the softening of the testicles, and the disease moves painfully when it wants to; and the cure for this disease is as effective as the previous one, and yet we will tell you its action according to what the ancients did.Li ancien disoient que l’on doit delivre li susdiz aposteme de toute tenve qui le confoint, et li coions aussi, selonc la similitude qu’il a a borjon, et delivre li testicoles de totes pars, et li suspensoire ausi.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	It is necessary for you to have the patient sit on an elevated seat, then tie the suspensory of testicles down with your fingers, to all the vessels that are close to the penis, and tie them tightly, and stretch them out properly; then cut through the vessels with a sharp knife in a straight line, so that they are exposed, and then scorch from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries in the temples; then insert a needle where there is a double thread, and tie it to the first place where the vein came, and tie it directly to the other end; then draw them gently according to the length of the body, and along the moistened vessels; then cure the wound as with the others, or with a bowstring, so that no vessel that nourishes one of the testicles is cut; for this does not cause harm, and if veins appear in all the vessels, then the testicles must be drawn at all the vessels; so that the oxygen does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and they dry out and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rotgut wound
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The occurrences of this hernia are through the opening that comes from the scrotum, or the extension over the abdomen in the region of the groin, causing the intestines to descend from this opening to one of the testicles; and this opening is in the scrotum, or from its extension, and these two types of hernias come from many causes: from percussion, or jumping, or coughing, or lifting a heavy load, and through similar actions. The sign that it is an extension from the scrotum is that it happens slowly over a long time, and does not come suddenly; and the hernia is even all the way to the bottom, because the scrotum presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is of the section of the sinus, that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and there are different abscesses appearing underneath the skin close to the surface, and it is due to the discharge of the intestines and the body from the sinus.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the fester comes with the intestines, and is retained inside, and causes great suffering to the patient, especially when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments using iron, there is fear, which is why one should avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement; et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz; puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz; puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars; puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne; et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi; et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant; puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	And the method of treatment is to instruct the patient to bring the intestine back inside through the wound with his hand, if he can; then hold his scrotum between your hands and lift the testicles; then press on the abdomen above them, and grab all the skin of the scrotum from the top; then insert your fingers into the opening of the groin according to what you need to open the wound, so that the intestinal loop can exit; then scrape the scrotum that is under the skin of the testicles, until the hard white scrotum is exposed all around; then insert your index finger into the space between the testicle and the scrotum, in the space between the white scrotum and the second testicle, and separate the one behind the testicle from the second testicle; then move your right hand inside the scrotum, and hold the white scrotum up with your left hand, and lift the testicle towards the abdomen, pulling it away from the scrotum; and instruct the assistant to extend the testicle upwards and loosen what is behind the ligature; then feel with your fingers if there is any intestinal loop wrapped around the hard white scrotum, and if you find anything, pull it back into the abdomen; then take a needle with a thick thread made of 10 threads, and insert it through the back part of the scrotum, which is after the skin of the testicles; then grab the ends of the threads that appear, until there are 4 threads; then tie them together in a cross-shape, and tie up the scrotum with a strong ligature in two places; then wrap the thread around the testicle, and tie it tightly in two places, so that none of the blood vessels that supply it can enter, so that no hernia occurs; then place the second ligature according to the first long ligature two fingers from it; and after these two ligatures, leave the scrotum that is under the testicles the width of a finger; then grab the part under the skin of the scrotum, as we said before, so that the blood vessels are cut off; then apply moist wool to the wound, and tie up the ligature as we have described.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have described is cauterized after the incision, due to doubt about blood flow.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece; puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	For this happens many times, and leave the bandage on until it bites through; and if it is slow to fall off, then use a hot water poultice, and apply what we have said above, until it drops off; then treat the wound with another treatment, until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz; puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the old ones said that it is made like the ramie fiber which is together with the thread, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after cutting above and below lightly; then cut them open halfway down, and treat the abscess with what was mentioned, until the vessels burst; then treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres; et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent; et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert; et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere: et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois; et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac; et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre; puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines; puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Sometimes the rot enters into the veins as mentioned, and opens up the area; and none of the intestines come out to the testicles, and if any do come out, it is a little bit, and it repairs itself every hour; and even if it remains too long in that state, it causes swelling and pain in the area where the intestines come out; and this happens because of the extension of the syphilis into the veins, as we have said, for it is stretched, then becomes soft and swollen and opens up; and its treatment is by cauterization, as we have said before; and sometimes it is treated by iron in the following manner: the patient lies on his back between your hands, then cut open the area of the rot with a broad knife according to the amount of three fingers; then draw out the syphilis which is under the skin that the sweat comes from, then take the thread and place it over the visible part of the syphilis; and press it deeply into the lower abdomen, then cut the two visible parts of the syphilis on the head of the thread, and cut both; then draw out the head of the thread, and do not cover or stretch the syphilis, nor anything else, as I have made you aware in the treatment of intestinal rot; then treat it by wound treatment.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, it cleans and cures the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	Syrup is constricting and has no appearance in the wound, and cautery is better for this purpose and closer to safety.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men, because the parts inside are softened, and it appears milky white; and when one wishes to treat this, he should make the patient lie on his back, and cut the softened skin on top of the natural skin; then bring together the two edges of the wound with a single stitch, and if you see that there is excess softened skin, sew it shut with three or four stitches firmly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it as you would other wounds until it heals, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	of chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	You should know that castration is forbidden in our law, and because of this, I would prefer not to discuss it in this book. However, knowledge of castration is necessary for two reasons: the first is so that doctors can answer questions about it and know how to perform the procedure; the second is because we often need to castrate certain animals to aid us, such as bulls, rams, goats, and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	I say, then, that castration is done in two ways: by attraction or by cutting.Car si on atract le membre qui est entre les deux testikols et li testikols, il est fait par atraction; et s’il est fendu, il est fais par fendure; et la fendeure doit être a l’enbas du membre et a l’enbas des testikols.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	In that which we do by traction, we cause the animal to sit in hot water until its joints are loosened and hanging; then squeeze them with your hand until they are reset and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	On the castration of the testicles: you should dye the animal and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cup each testicle in turn, once you have well-scrotched them; and leave some powder of the simple syrup and the subtle syrup which is on the vessels; and this manner of castration is better than that which is done by traction, because with traction something may remain in the testicles, causing the animal to desire lust; then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways in men: one is that between the testicles there appears what looks like a woman's genitals, with hair, and sometimes it even discharges urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other method is for women, and it has on the buttock a rod-like protuberance and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	And the treatment for men and women is to treat the hernias as you would any other hernia; but in the second type of hernia in men where the urine exits through the scrotum, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	A hernia is a swelling above the natural opening, so large that it is ugly to behold; some women have them as big as a hand, and that is the treatment for them.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	You should dye the excess of the hernia with your hand or fingernails, and cup it gently; do not push too hard or blood will come out, then treat the other hernia until it is healed; and for another type that exits at the mouth of the anus, use a mixture of honey and vinegar, and perhaps it will disappear, and it is like a pustule, and so they call it "cow's disease.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you must treat it, as we have said, with cautery, and heal it until it is cured.
de erratique	of erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	It is errant if the nature of the woman is not understood, or the passage is small; and it is natural from birth, or accidental due to illness that comes to it; or it is due to a foreign object, or a ulcerous or thick growth, and it is formed as a deep cavity in the womb, or in the sides, or below, or wherever; and they should understand conception and childbirth, and perhaps flowers to have; and the knowledge of this is through the examination of the vagina.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the tumors are visible nearby, then use your fingers or a probe.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	If it is from a ulcerous growth and it is nearby the lips, then do this: place your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread; then form the lips, so that the ulcerous growth is pushed in, and cover the tumor; then take wool, moisten it in oil, and place it over the area, and have the woman lie at home every day so that it may not heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the ulcer is hard and thick, then you must cut it with a spatulum like a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound is from a fresh cut, then stop the bleeding and apply medicine to stop the bleeding, such as dragon's blood, incense, and egg white; then take a large piece of wool so that the wound does not close; then let it be for a long time, and apply a dressing of dry linen; then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when there is fresh blood in a wound, it must be covered in this way, unless it is an abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For one must not cut into an abscess that is in the breast.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	Hemorrhoids are veins that open without custom, and when hemorrhoids are old they become התלול (telul, meaning 'steep' or 'perpendicular'). We have already described their appearances, signs, and treatments in the section on wounds.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and thrombosed external hemorrhoids, when they are perfectly formed in the anus and do not appear on examination, are not cured by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those which are at the mouth of the anus, one can feel; these can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	Therefore, you should put the woman in a cold room; then, use tweezers to remove the hemorrhoids at their roots and powder them with medicines that constrict blood vessels, such as acacia, dragon's blood, incense, and similar substances; then, bind her feet to the wall for an hour, then place her in cold water. If there is any discharge of blood, have her sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate bark, galls, and similar ingredients. Then take barley flour, mix it with honey and garlic, and make a poultice out of it to apply to her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it is stopped up, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.
